206                 *(\hyperlink{openavb__types__base__pub_8h_a696390429f2f3b644bde8d0322a24124}{U32} *)&(pRsp->\hyperlink{structopenavb__aecp__response__data__get__counters__t_a42270fad37ed864105800158dfdbbf54}{counters\_block}[
      \hyperlink{openavb__aecp__cmd__get__counters_8h_a4d7cfced872e8a2681516f3080b2aa61}{OPENAVB\_AEM\_GET\_COUNTERS\_COMMAND\_STREAM\_INPUT\_OFFSET\_EARLY\_TIMESTAMP}
      ]) = htonl(value);
207             \}
208             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (\hyperlink{openavb__avdecc__pipeline__interaction__pub_8h_a9e5fd33f021a94e43f62ae4b0793ccdc}{openavbAVDECCGetCounterValue}(pDescriptorStreamInput, 
      \hyperlink{openavb__aem__types__pub_8h_a5e3af66c16a6e4af6d5d3422f372be55}{OPENAVB\_AEM\_DESCRIPTOR\_STREAM\_INPUT}, 
      \hyperlink{openavb__aem__types__pub_8h_a43ac84d24d277f3ea088d00a63b77f16}{OPENAVB\_AEM\_GET\_COUNTERS\_COMMAND\_STREAM\_INPUT\_COUNTER\_FRAMES\_RX}
      , &value)) \{
209                 pRsp->\hyperlink{structopenavb__aecp__response__data__get__counters__t_a65aa742a6a13f1f3df23d7f0e50901ec}{counters\_valid} |= 
      \hyperlink{openavb__aem__types__pub_8h_a43ac84d24d277f3ea088d00a63b77f16}{OPENAVB\_AEM\_GET\_COUNTERS\_COMMAND\_STREAM\_INPUT\_COUNTER\_FRAMES\_RX}
      ;
210                 *(\hyperlink{openavb__types__base__pub_8h_a696390429f2f3b644bde8d0322a24124}{U32} *)&(pRsp->\hyperlink{structopenavb__aecp__response__data__get__counters__t_a42270fad37ed864105800158dfdbbf54}{counters\_block}[
      \hyperlink{openavb__aecp__cmd__get__counters_8h_a0c84819591d595a31a9aa373607bac15}{OPENAVB\_AEM\_GET\_COUNTERS\_COMMAND\_STREAM\_INPUT\_OFFSET\_FRAMES\_RX}
      ]) = htonl(value);
211             \}
212             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (\hyperlink{openavb__avdecc__pipeline__interaction__pub_8h_a9e5fd33f021a94e43f62ae4b0793ccdc}{openavbAVDECCGetCounterValue}(pDescriptorStreamInput, 
      \hyperlink{openavb__aem__types__pub_8h_a5e3af66c16a6e4af6d5d3422f372be55}{OPENAVB\_AEM\_DESCRIPTOR\_STREAM\_INPUT}, 
      \hyperlink{openavb__aem__types__pub_8h_ad41202322f8df5127d4b49113220c55d}{OPENAVB\_AEM\_GET\_COUNTERS\_COMMAND\_STREAM\_INPUT\_COUNTER\_FRAMES\_TX}
      , &value)) \{
213                 pRsp->\hyperlink{structopenavb__aecp__response__data__get__counters__t_a65aa742a6a13f1f3df23d7f0e50901ec}{counters\_valid} |= 
      \hyperlink{openavb__aem__types__pub_8h_ad41202322f8df5127d4b49113220c55d}{OPENAVB\_AEM\_GET\_COUNTERS\_COMMAND\_STREAM\_INPUT\_COUNTER\_FRAMES\_TX}
      ;
214                 *(\hyperlink{openavb__types__base__pub_8h_a696390429f2f3b644bde8d0322a24124}{U32} *)&(pRsp->\hyperlink{structopenavb__aecp__response__data__get__counters__t_a42270fad37ed864105800158dfdbbf54}{counters\_block}[
      \hyperlink{openavb__aecp__cmd__get__counters_8h_af619feaea38135ccbbf0a9a284aa67db}{OPENAVB\_AEM\_GET\_COUNTERS\_COMMAND\_STREAM\_INPUT\_OFFSET\_FRAMES\_TX}
      ]) = htonl(value);
215             \}
216             \hyperlink{openavb__aecp__cmd__get__counters_8c_a18c1fc6e24fc63b04f0a2cbd88a9b8d2}{GetEntitySpecificCounters}(pDescriptorStreamInput, 
      \hyperlink{openavb__aem__types__pub_8h_a5e3af66c16a6e4af6d5d3422f372be55}{OPENAVB\_AEM\_DESCRIPTOR\_STREAM\_INPUT}, pRsp);
217 
218             result = \hyperlink{openavb__aem__types__pub_8h_acce02f99784692c62e00b4a40ee715a3}{OPENAVB\_AEM\_COMMAND\_STATUS\_SUCCESS};
219         \}
220     \}
221 
222     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} result;
223 \}
\end{DoxyCode}
